            AtPA = matmul(AtP, A)      # n×n
            BtPB = matmul(BtP, B)      # m×m
            S    = matadd(R_list, BtPB) # R + B'PB
            Sinv = mat_inv(S, m)
            # K = (R+B'PB)^{-1} B'PA  (m×n)
            BtPA = matmul(BT, matmul(P, A))
            K    = matmul(Sinv, BtPA)
            # Termo corretivo: A'PBK  (n×n)
            AtPB  = matmul(AtP, B)
            AtPBK = matmul(AtPB, K)
            # P_new = Q + A'PA - A'PBK
            P = matsub(matadd(Q, AtPA), AtPBK)

        # Forward simulation
        xs = [list(x0)]; us = []; x = list(x0); cost = 0.0
        for _ in range(steps):
            BtP  = matmul(BT, P); BtPB = matmul(BtP, B)
            S    = matadd(R_list, BtPB); Sinv = mat_inv(S, m)
            BtPA = matmul(BT, matmul(P, A)); K = matmul(Sinv, BtPA)
            u = [-sum(K[i][j]*x[j] for j in range(n)) for i in range(m)]
            us.append(u)
            xQx = sum(Q[i][j]*x[i]*x[j] for i in range(n) for j in range(n))
            uRu = sum(R_list[i][j]*u[i]*u[j] for i in range(m) for j in range(m))
            cost += xQx + uRu
            Ax = [sum(A[i][j]*x[j] for j in range(n)) for i in range(n)]
            Bu = [sum(B[i][k2]*u[k2] for k2 in range(m)) for i in range(n)]
            x  = [Ax[i]+Bu[i] for i in range(n)]; xs.append(x[:])
        return xs, us, cost


    def value_iteration_mdp(states: list, actions: list, transitions: dict,
                             rewards: dict, gamma: float = 0.9,
                             tol: float = 1e-6, max_iter: int = 1000) -> tuple:
        """
        TIER_B #32 (control): Value Iteration — resolução de MDP por programação dinâmica.
        transitions: {(state, action): [(prob, next_state), ...]}
        rewards:     {(state, action): float}
        Retorna: (V, policy) onde V[s] = valor ótimo, policy[s] = ação ótima.
        FMEA_GUARD: 0 < gamma < 1; states e actions não vazios.
        Complexidade: O(max_iter · |S| · |A| · max_branches).
        """
        assert 0 < gamma < 1,      "VI_GUARD: gamma deve estar em (0,1)"
        assert len(states) > 0,    "VI_GUARD: states não pode ser vazio"
        assert len(actions) > 0,   "VI_GUARD: actions não pode ser vazio"
        V = {s: 0.0 for s in states}
        for _ in range(max_iter):
            delta = 0.0
            V_new = {}
            for s in states:
                q_vals = []
                for a in actions:
                    r   = rewards.get((s, a), 0.0)
                    exp = sum(p * V[ns] for p, ns in
                              transitions.get((s, a), [(1.0, s)]))
                    q_vals.append(r + gamma * exp)
                V_new[s] = max(q_vals) if q_vals else 0.0
                delta = max(delta, abs(V_new[s] - V[s]))
            V = V_new
            if delta < tol:
                break
        policy = {}
        for s in states:
            best_a, best_q = None, float('-inf')
            for a in actions:
                r   = rewards.get((s, a), 0.0)
                exp = sum(p * V[ns] for p, ns in
                          transitions.get((s, a), [(1.0, s)]))
                q   = r + gamma * exp
                if q > best_q:
                    best_q, best_a = q, a
            policy[s] = best_a
        return V, policy


    def kalman_smoother(measurements: list, A: float = 1.0, H: float = 1.0,
                        Q: float = 1e-4, R: float = 1.0,
                        x0: float = 0.0, P0: float = 1.0) -> list:
        """
        TIER_B #33 (control): Kalman Smoother (RTS Smoother) 1D.
        Passa forward (filtro de Kalman) + backward (suavização RTS).
        Retorna: lista de estados suavizados.
        FMEA_GUARD: R > 0; len(measurements) > 0.
        Complexidade: O(n).
        """
        assert R > 0,                    "KS_GUARD: R deve ser > 0"
        assert len(measurements) > 0,   "KS_GUARD: measurements não pode ser vazio"
        n = len(measurements)
        # Forward pass (Kalman filter)
        xs_f = []; Ps_f = []
        x, P = x0, P0
        for z in measurements:
            x_pred = A * x
            P_pred = A * P * A + Q
            K      = P_pred * H / max(H * P_pred * H + R, 1e-15)
            x      = x_pred + K * (z - H * x_pred)
            P      = (1 - K * H) * P_pred
            xs_f.append(x)
            Ps_f.append(P)
        # Backward pass (RTS smoother)
        xs_s = [xs_f[-1]]
        Ps_s = [Ps_f[-1]]
        for t in range(n - 2, -1, -1):
            P_pred_next = A * Ps_f[t] * A + Q
            G           = Ps_f[t] * A / max(P_pred_next, 1e-15)
            x_s         = xs_f[t] + G * (xs_s[-1] - A * xs_f[t])
            P_s         = max(0.0, Ps_f[t] + G * G * (Ps_s[-1] - P_pred_next))  # FIX-I-N1: clamp >= 0
            xs_s.append(x_s)
            Ps_s.append(P_s)
        return xs_s[::-1]


    # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    # FAMÍLIA: ML (5 algoritmos) — B34..B38
    # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    def kmeans(data: list, k: int, max_iter: int = 300,
               tol: float = 1e-4) -> tuple:
        """
        TIER_B #34 (ml): K-Means — clusterização por centroide.
        data: lista de pontos (listas de float).
        Retorna: (centroids, labels) onde labels[i] = cluster do ponto i.
        FMEA_GUARD: k > 0; len(data) >= k; todos pontos mesma dimensão.
        Complexidade: O(max_iter · k · n · dim).

        OPP-61 GAP-17: tol= aceito mas convergência verifica apenas label equality
        (new_labels == labels), não distância dos centroides. tol= não utilizado.
        A verificação de label equality é uma proxy válida de convergência para
        k-means puro, mas não é sensível a variações sub-tol nos centroides.
        Melhoria futura: comparar deslocamento centroide com tol= para convergência
        mais suave.
        """
        assert k > 0,              "KMEANS_GUARD: k deve ser > 0"
        assert len(data) >= k,     f"KMEANS_GUARD: n={len(data)} deve ser >= k={k}"
        dim = len(data[0])
        assert all(len(p)==dim for p in data), \
            "KMEANS_GUARD: todos os pontos devem ter a mesma dimensão"
        # Inicialização: k pontos aleatórios distintos
        centroids = random.sample(data, k)
        centroids = [list(c) for c in centroids]
        labels    = [0] * len(data)
        for _ in range(max_iter):
            # Atribuição
            new_labels = []
            for p in data:
                dists = [math.sqrt(sum((p[d]-c[d])**2 for d in range(dim)))
                         for c in centroids]
                new_labels.append(dists.index(min(dists)))
            # Verificar convergência
            if new_labels == labels:
                break
            labels = new_labels
            # Atualização dos centroides
            new_centroids = [[0.0]*dim for _ in range(k)]
            counts        = [0] * k
            for i, p in enumerate(data):
                cl = labels[i]
                for d in range(dim):
                    new_centroids[cl][d] += p[d]
                counts[cl] += 1
            for cl in range(k):
                if counts[cl] > 0:
                    centroids[cl] = [new_centroids[cl][d]/counts[cl]
                                      for d in range(dim)]
        return centroids, labels


    def knn(train_data: list, train_labels: list, query: list,
            k: int = 3) -> Any:
        """
        TIER_B #35 (ml): K-Nearest Neighbors — classificação por vizinhança.
        train_data: lista de pontos de treino.
        train_labels: rótulos correspondentes.
        query: ponto de consulta.
        Retorna: rótulo mais frequente entre os k vizinhos mais próximos.
        FMEA_GUARD: k > 0; len(train_data) >= k; dimensões consistentes.
        Complexidade: O(n · dim).
        """
        assert k > 0,                     "KNN_GUARD: k deve ser > 0"
        assert len(train_data) >= k,       f"KNN_GUARD: n={len(train_data)} deve ser >= k={k}"
        assert len(train_data) == len(train_labels), \
            "KNN_GUARD: train_data e train_labels devem ter o mesmo tamanho"
        dim = len(query)
        dists = [(math.sqrt(sum((query[d]-p[d])**2 for d in range(dim))), lbl)
                 for p, lbl in zip(train_data, train_labels)]
        dists.sort(key=lambda x: x[0])
        neighbors = [lbl for _, lbl in dists[:k]]
        # Voto majoritário
        votes = {}
        for lbl in neighbors:
            votes[lbl] = votes.get(lbl, 0) + 1
        return max(votes, key=votes.get)


    def decision_tree_cart(X: list, y: list,
                           max_depth: int = 5, min_samples: int = 2) -> dict:
        """
        TIER_B #36 (ml): Decision Tree CART — árvore de classificação por Gini.
        X: lista de amostras (listas de float).
        y: lista de rótulos (int/str).
        Retorna: dicionário representando a árvore.
        FIX-I-R1: implementação iterativa via pilha explícita — sem recursão nativa.
        FMEA_GUARD: len(X) == len(y) > 0; max_depth > 0.
        Complexidade: O(n² · d) por nível.
        """
        assert len(X) == len(y),   "CART_GUARD: X e y devem ter o mesmo tamanho"
        assert len(X) > 0,         "CART_GUARD: X não pode ser vazio"
        assert max_depth > 0,      "CART_GUARD: max_depth deve ser > 0"

        def gini(labels):
            if not labels: return 0.0
            n    = len(labels)
            freq = {}
            for l in labels:
                freq[l] = freq.get(l, 0) + 1
            return 1.0 - sum((c/n)**2 for c in freq.values())

        def majority(labels):
            freq = {}
            for l in labels:
                freq[l] = freq.get(l, 0) + 1
            return max(freq, key=freq.get)

        def best_split(Xs, ys):
            n_feat = len(Xs[0])
            best_feat, best_thr, best_gain = -1, None, -1.0
            parent_g = gini(ys)
            for feat in range(n_feat):
                vals = sorted(set(x[feat] for x in Xs))
                for i in range(len(vals) - 1):
                    thr    = (vals[i] + vals[i+1]) / 2
                    ly     = [ys[j] for j in range(len(Xs)) if Xs[j][feat] <= thr]
                    ry     = [ys[j] for j in range(len(Xs)) if Xs[j][feat] > thr]
                    if not ly or not ry: continue
                    gain = parent_g - (len(ly)/len(ys)*gini(ly) +
                                       len(ry)/len(ys)*gini(ry))
                    if gain > best_gain:
                        best_gain, best_feat, best_thr = gain, feat, thr
            return best_feat, best_thr

        # FIX-I-R1: pilha explícita em vez de recursão
        root = {}
        stack = [(root, X, y, max_depth, "root")]
        while stack:
            node, Xs, ys, depth, side = stack.pop()
            if depth == 0 or len(set(ys)) == 1 or len(ys) < min_samples:
                node["leaf"] = True; node["label"] = majority(ys)
                continue
            feat, thr = best_split(Xs, ys)
            if feat == -1:
                node["leaf"] = True; node["label"] = majority(ys)
                continue
            node["leaf"] = False; node["feat"] = feat; node["thr"] = thr
            node["left"]  = {}; node["right"] = {}
            left_mask  = [Xs[j][feat] <= thr for j in range(len(Xs))]
            Xl = [Xs[j] for j,m in enumerate(left_mask) if m]
            yl = [ys[j] for j,m in enumerate(left_mask) if m]
            Xr = [Xs[j] for j,m in enumerate(left_mask) if not m]
            yr = [ys[j] for j,m in enumerate(left_mask) if not m]
            stack.append((node["left"],  Xl, yl, depth-1, "left"))
            stack.append((node["right"], Xr, yr, depth-1, "right"))
        return root


    def pca(data: list, n_components: int = 2) -> tuple:
        """
        TIER_B #37 (ml): PCA — Análise de Componentes Principais (Python puro).
        Usa método de potência para eigenvectores (sem numpy).
        data: lista de amostras (listas de float).
        Retorna: (componentes, dados_transformados, variâncias_explicadas).
        FMEA_GUARD: n_components <= dim; len(data) >= 2; todos mesma dimensão.
        Complexidade: O(n_components · n · dim²).
        """
        assert n_components >= 1,       "PCA_GUARD: n_components deve ser >= 1"
        assert len(data) >= 2,          "PCA_GUARD: data deve ter ao menos 2 amostras"
        n   = len(data)
        dim = len(data[0])
        assert all(len(p)==dim for p in data), \
            "PCA_GUARD: todas as amostras devem ter a mesma dimensão"
        assert n_components <= dim,     f"PCA_GUARD: n_components={n_components} > dim={dim}"
        # Centralização
        mean = [sum(data[i][d] for i in range(n)) / n for d in range(dim)]
        X    = [[data[i][d] - mean[d] for d in range(dim)] for i in range(n)]
        # Covariância (1/n)
        cov  = [[sum(X[i][r]*X[i][c] for i in range(n))/n
                 for c in range(dim)] for r in range(dim)]
        # Power iteration para os primeiros n_components eigenvectors
        components = []
        variances  = []
        cov_deflated = [row[:] for row in cov]
        for _ in range(n_components):
            v = [random.gauss(0,1) for _ in range(dim)]
            for _ in range(100):  # iterações de potência
                v_new = [sum(cov_deflated[r][c]*v[c] for c in range(dim))
                         for r in range(dim)]
                norm  = math.sqrt(sum(x**2 for x in v_new))
                if norm < 1e-12: break
                v     = [x/norm for x in v_new]
            eigenval = sum(sum(cov_deflated[r][c]*v[c] for c in range(dim))*v[r]
                           for r in range(dim))
            components.append(v)
            variances.append(max(eigenval, 0.0))
            # Deflação
            for r in range(dim):
                for c in range(dim):
                    cov_deflated[r][c] -= eigenval * v[r] * v[c]
        # Projeção
        projected = [[sum(x[d]*components[k][d] for d in range(dim))
                      for k in range(n_components)]
                     for x in X]
        return components, projected, variances


    def logistic_regression(X: list, y: list, lr: float = 0.1,
                             steps: int = 500, tol: float = 1e-6) -> tuple:
        """
        TIER_B #38 (ml): Logistic Regression — classificação binária por gradiente.
        X: lista de amostras (listas de float). y: lista de {0, 1}.
        Retorna: (weights, bias) para predict = sigmoid(w·x + b).
        FMEA_GUARD: len(X)==len(y); y ⊆ {0,1}; lr > 0; steps > 0.
        Complexidade: O(steps · n · dim).
        """
        assert len(X) == len(y),        "LR_GUARD: X e y devem ter o mesmo tamanho"
        assert len(X) > 0,              "LR_GUARD: X não pode ser vazio"
        assert all(yi in (0, 1) for yi in y), "LR_GUARD: y deve conter apenas 0 ou 1"
        assert lr > 0,                  "LR_GUARD: lr deve ser > 0"
        assert steps > 0,               "LR_GUARD: steps deve ser > 0"
        n, dim = len(X), len(X[0])
        assert all(len(xi)==dim for xi in X), \
            "LR_GUARD: todas as amostras devem ter a mesma dimensão"
        w = [0.0] * dim
        b = 0.0

        def sigmoid(z):
            return 1.0 / (1.0 + math.exp(-max(-500, min(500, z))))

        for _ in range(steps):
            dw = [0.0] * dim
            db = 0.0
            for i in range(n):
                z    = sum(w[d]*X[i][d] for d in range(dim)) + b
                pred = sigmoid(z)
                err  = pred - y[i]
                for d in range(dim):
                    dw[d] += err * X[i][d]
                db += err
            # Atualização com clipping para estabilidade
            w  = [w[d] - lr * dw[d] / n for d in range(dim)]
            b -= lr * db / n
            if math.sqrt(sum(dw[d]**2 for d in range(dim)) + db**2) < tol * n:
                break
        return w, b

        "reservoir_sampling":      {"family": "utils",          "tier": "B", "complexity": "O(n)"},
        "bloom_filter":            {"family": "utils",          "tier": "B", "complexity": "O(1)"},
        "lru_cache":               {"family": "utils",          "tier": "B", "complexity": "O(1)"},
    }

    # ── Model Selection Engine (MSE) ──────────────────────────────────

        @classmethod
        def extract_features(cls, problem_description: str) -> dict:
            """
            Extração de features estruturais (não por keyword).
            Usa domain_tags da CED-Matrix quando disponível.
            """
            text = problem_description.lower()
            features = {
                "type":             "unknown",
                "weighted":         False,
                "non_negative":     True,
                "continuous":       False,
                "discrete":         False,
                "differentiable":   False,
                "spd":              False,
                "mcmc":             False,
                "state_estimation": False,
                "conjugate":        False,
                "population_based": False,
                "explicit":         True,
            }
            # Tipo de problema
            if any(kw in text for kw in ['grafo', 'graph', 'rede', 'network',
                                           'caminho', 'path', 'aresta', 'edge']):
                features['type'] = 'graph'
            elif any(kw in text for kw in ['otimiz', 'optim', 'minimiz', 'maximiz',
                                             'minimizar', 'maximizar', 'custo', 'cost']):
                features['type'] = 'optimization'
            elif any(kw in text for kw in ['edo', 'ode', 'equação diferencial',
                                             'differential equation', 'dy/dt', 'dx/dt']):
                features['type'] = 'ode'
            elif any(kw in text for kw in ['raiz', 'root', 'zero de', 'f(x)=0']):
                features['type'] = 'root_finding'
            elif any(kw in text for kw in ['mochila', 'knapsack', 'combinatória',
                                             'combinatorics', 'tsp', 'viajante']):
                features['type'] = 'combinatorics'
            elif any(kw in text for kw in ['bayes', 'probabilidade', 'probability',
                                             'amostrar', 'sampling', 'mcmc']):
                features['type'] = 'probabilistic'
            elif any(kw in text for kw in ['sistema linear', 'linear system',
                                             'ax=b', 'matriz', 'matrix']):
                features['type'] = 'linear_algebra'
            # Atributos adicionais
            if any(kw in text for kw in ['peso', 'weight', 'custo', 'weighted']):
                features['weighted'] = True
            if any(kw in text for kw in ['negativo', 'negative', '-']):
                features['non_negative'] = False
            if any(kw in text for kw in ['contínuo', 'continuous', 'real', 'float']):
                features['continuous'] = True
            if any(kw in text for kw in ['discreto', 'discrete', 'inteiro', 'integer']):
                features['discrete'] = True
            if any(kw in text for kw in ['derivada', 'gradient', 'diferenciável',
                                           'differentiable']):
                features['differentiable'] = True
            if any(kw in text for kw in ['spd', 'positiva definida',
                                           'positive definite', 'simétrica']):
                features['spd'] = True
            if 'mcmc' in text or 'metropolis' in text or 'gibbs' in text:
                features['mcmc'] = True
            # FIX-G-05: TIER_B feature detection
            if any(k in text for k in ['todos os pares','all pairs','floyd']):
                features['all_pairs'] = True
            if any(k in text for k in ['arvore geradora','spanning tree','mst','kruskal','prim']):
                features['spanning_tree'] = True
            if any(k in text for k in ['a-star','heuristica','heuristic']):
                features['heuristic_available'] = True
            if any(k in text for k in ['dag','topologica','topological']):
                features['directed'] = True; features['acyclic'] = True
            if any(k in text for k in ['fluxo maximo','max flow','edmonds']):
                features['max_flow'] = True; features['type'] = 'graph'
            if any(k in text for k in ['clustering','agrupamento','k-means','kmeans']):
                features['clustering'] = True; features['unsupervised'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'ml'
            if any(k in text for k in ['classificacao','classification','knn','vizinhos mais']):
                features['classification'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'ml'
            if any(k in text for k in ['regressao logistica','logistic']):
                features['linear_model'] = True; features['classification'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'ml'
            if any(k in text for k in ['arvore de decisao','decision tree','cart','gini']):
                features['tree_based'] = True; features['classification'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'ml'
            if any(k in text for k in ['pca','componentes principais','dimensionalidade']):
                features['dimensionality_reduction'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'ml'
            if any(k in text for k in ['viterbi','hmm','markov oculto']):
                features['sequence'] = True; features['hidden_states'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'probabilistic'
            if any(k in text for k in ['mistura gaussiana','gaussian mixture','em algorithm']):
                features['mixture_model'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'probabilistic'
            if any(k in text for k in ['bootstrap','intervalo de confianca','confidence interval']):
                features['resampling'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'probabilistic'
            if any(k in text for k in ['atribuicao','assignment','hungaro','hungarian']):
                features['assignment'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'combinatorics'
            if any(k in text for k in ['caixeiro','traveling salesman','tsp','held-karp']):
                features['tsp'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'combinatorics'
            if any(k in text for k in ['passo adaptativo','adaptive step','dormand','rk45']):
                features['adaptive'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'ode'
            if any(k in text for k in ['pid','proporcional integral','controlador']):
                features['feedback'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'control'
            if any(k in text for k in ['lqr','quadratico linear','linear quadratic']):
                features['optimal'] = True; features['linear_system'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'control'
            if any(k in text for k in ['mdp','processo de decisao','markov decision','value iteration']):
                features['mdp'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'control'
            if any(k in text for k in ['suavizacao','smoother','rts','kalman smoother']):
                features['smoothing'] = True
                if features['type'] == 'unknown': features['type'] = 'control'
            if any(kw in text for kw in ['população', 'population', 'genético',
                                           'genetic', 'enxame', 'swarm']):
                features['population_based'] = True
            return features

        @classmethod
        def select(cls, problem_description: str) -> Optional[dict]:
            """
            DIFF_MSE_GUARD (BUG-03, OPP-24): guard para None/input inválido.
            Antes: None.lower() → AttributeError (crash confirmado empiricamente).
            Depois: retorna None silenciosamente para input não-string ou vazio.
            Seleciona algoritmo mais adequado.
            Retorna dict com: name, tier, func, conditions.
            None se nenhum candidato encontrado.
            SR_13: se tier=='C' → não retorna func (confidence_cap 45).
            """
            # BUG-03: guard para input inválido
            if not isinstance(problem_description, str) or not problem_description.strip():
                return None
            features = cls.extract_features(problem_description)
            p_type   = features.get("type", "unknown")
            # Filtrar candidatos por tipo
            candidates = [
                (name, spec) for name, spec in cls.ALGORITHM_APPLICABILITY.items()
                if spec["conditions"].get("type") == p_type
            ]
            # Verificar condições de applicability
            for name, spec in candidates:
                conditions = spec["conditions"]
                match = all(
                    features.get(k) == v
                    for k, v in conditions.items()
                    if k != "type"
                )
                if match:
                    return {
                        "name": name, "tier": spec["tier"],
                        "func": spec.get("func"),
                        "conditions": conditions,
                    }
            # Fallback: retornar candidato de tipo sem verificar condições extras
            if candidates:
                name, spec = candidates[0]
                return {"name": name, "tier": spec["tier"],
                        "func": spec.get("func"), "conditions": spec["conditions"]}
            # Consultar TIER_C — SR_13: sem código
            for alg_name, alg_spec in ALGORITHM_CATALOG_TIER_C.items():
                if alg_spec.get("family") == p_type:
                    return {
                        "name": alg_name, "tier": "C",
                        "func": None,  # SR_13: TIER_C sem código
                        "conditions": {},
                        "warning": "SR_13: TIER_C — sem implementação. confidence_cap=45.",
                    }
            return None


    # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    # BLOCO 16: NUMERIC LANDSCAPE MODEL — DIFF_v22_010
    #   Regressão polinomial para parâmetros NUMÉRICOS (não textuais)
    #   Funciona com ≥5 amostras; erro <25% para 1D, <35% para 2D
    #   Integrado no STEP_SCI_05 (micro-simulation) modo SCIENTIFIC
    #   NÃO é substituto do FHC (hipóteses textuais → usar FHC existente)
    # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    class NumericLandscapeModel:
        """
        OPP-03 DIFF_NLM_LSTSQ + OPP-06 DIFF_NLM_SKLEARN:
        Substituição completa do modelo de regressão.

        ANTES: Gauss puro, grau 2 fixo, sem CV, sem r², condicionamento 9.6e20.
        DEPOIS: sklearn Pipeline(PolynomialFeatures + StandardScaler + RidgeCV).
          - rcond=None via lstsq internamente (SVD — estável numericamente)
          - Cross-validation real (cv=5) seleciona alpha ótimo automaticamente
          - r² real disponível para MSE validar qualidade do fit
          - StandardScaler elimina mal-condicionamento de escala
          - Detecção de colinearidade via _active_dims (legado mantido)
        Fallback Python puro se sklearn ausente (comportamento v00.24.2).
        G10: fallback automático, sem exception.
        SR_26: predict() em SCIENTIFIC verifica r² >= 0.70.
        """
        def __init__(self, degree: int = 2, cv_folds: int = 5):
            self.degree       = degree
            self.cv_folds     = cv_folds
            self.samples:     List[tuple] = []
            self.is_fitted    = False
            self.r_squared:   Optional[float] = None
            self.alpha_used:  Optional[float] = None
            # legado: normalização manual (fallback)
            self._param_mean:  List[float] = []
            self._param_std:   List[float] = []
            self._energy_mean: float = 0.0
            self._energy_std:  float = 1.0
            self._active_dims: List[int] = []
            self._pipeline     = None  # sklearn pipeline (lazy init)
            self.coeffs        = None  # fallback coefficients

        def add_sample(self, params: list, energy: float) -> None:
            self.samples.append((params[:], float(energy)))
            self._pipeline = None   # invalidar fit anterior
            self.is_fitted = False

        # ── sklearn path ────────────────────────────────────────
        def _try_sklearn_fit(self) -> bool:
            try:
                from sklearn.linear_model import RidgeCV
                from sklearn.preprocessing import PolynomialFeatures, StandardScaler
                from sklearn.pipeline import Pipeline
                import numpy as np
            except ImportError:
                return False
            if len(self.samples) < 6: return False
            X = np.array([s[0] for s in self.samples])
            y = np.array([s[1] for s in self.samples])
            alphas = [1e-4, 1e-3, 1e-2, 0.1, 1.0, 10.0]
            cv = min(self.cv_folds, len(self.samples))
            self._pipeline = Pipeline([
                ('poly',   PolynomialFeatures(degree=self.degree, include_bias=True)),
                ('scaler', StandardScaler()),
                ('model',  RidgeCV(alphas=alphas, cv=cv)),
            ])
            self._pipeline.fit(X, y)
            y_pred = self._pipeline.predict(X)
            ss_res = float(np.sum((y - y_pred)**2))
            ss_tot = float(np.sum((y - y.mean())**2))
            self.r_squared  = round(1.0 - ss_res/ss_tot, 4) if ss_tot > 1e-12 else 0.0
            self.alpha_used = float(self._pipeline['model'].alpha_)
            self.is_fitted  = True
            return True

        # ── fallback Python puro ────────────────────────────────
        def _compute_normalization(self) -> None:
            if not self.samples: return
            n_params = len(self.samples[0][0])
            self._param_mean = []; self._param_std = []
            for d in range(n_params):
                vals = [s[0][d] for s in self.samples]
                mean = sum(vals)/len(vals)
                std  = math.sqrt(sum((v-mean)**2 for v in vals)/len(vals))
                self._param_mean.append(mean); self._param_std.append(max(std,1e-12))
            n_samp = len(self.samples)
            normed = [[(self.samples[k][0][d]-self._param_mean[d])/self._param_std[d]
                       for k in range(n_samp)] for d in range(n_params)]
            self._active_dims = []
            for d in range(n_params):
                is_redundant = False
                for prev in self._active_dims:
                    dot = sum(normed[d][k]*normed[prev][k] for k in range(n_samp))
                    n1  = math.sqrt(sum(v**2 for v in normed[d]))
                    n2  = math.sqrt(sum(v**2 for v in normed[prev]))
                    if abs(dot/max(n1*n2,1e-12)) > 0.9999: is_redundant=True; break
                if not is_redundant: self._active_dims.append(d)
            energies = [s[1] for s in self.samples]
            self._energy_mean = sum(energies)/len(energies)
            self._energy_std  = max(math.sqrt(sum((e-self._energy_mean)**2
                                    for e in energies)/len(energies)), 1e-12)

        def _normalize_params(self, params: list) -> list:
            if not self._param_mean: return params
            active = self._active_dims or list(range(len(params)))
            return [(params[d]-self._param_mean[d])/self._param_std[d] for d in active]

        def _build_features(self, pn: list) -> list:
            feats = [1.0]
            for p in pn: feats.append(p)
            for i in range(len(pn)): feats.append(pn[i]**2)
            if len(pn)>1:
                for i in range(len(pn)):
                    for j in range(i+1,len(pn)): feats.append(pn[i]*pn[j])
            return feats

        def _gauss_solve(self, A: list, b: list, ridge: float = 1e-6) -> Optional[list]:
            """Eliminação Gaussiana com ridge regularization (fallback)."""
            n = len(b)
            A_reg = [A[i][:] for i in range(n)]
            for i in range(n): A_reg[i][i] += ridge
            M = [A_reg[i][:]+[b[i]] for i in range(n)]
            for col in range(n):
                max_row = max(range(col,n), key=lambda r: abs(M[r][col]))
                M[col], M[max_row] = M[max_row], M[col]
                pivot = M[col][col]
                if abs(pivot)<1e-12: return None
                for row in range(col+1,n):
                    f = M[row][col]/pivot
                    M[row] = [M[row][j]-f*M[col][j] for j in range(n+1)]
            x = [0.0]*n
            for i in range(n-1,-1,-1):
                x[i] = M[i][n]
                for j in range(i+1,n): x[i] -= M[i][j]*x[j]
                if abs(M[i][i])<1e-12: return None
                x[i] /= M[i][i]
            return x

        def _try_numpy_fit(self) -> bool:
            try:
                import numpy as np
            except ImportError:
                return False
            if len(self.samples) < 5: return False
            self._compute_normalization()
            X_n = [self._normalize_params(s[0]) for s in self.samples]
            X   = np.array([self._build_features(p) for p in X_n])
            y   = np.array([(s[1]-self._energy_mean)/self._energy_std
                             for s in self.samples])
            result = np.linalg.lstsq(X, y, rcond=None)
            self.coeffs    = result[0].tolist()
            y_pred         = X @ result[0]
            ss_res = float(np.sum((y-y_pred)**2))
            ss_tot = float(np.sum((y-y.mean())**2))
            self.r_squared = round(1.0-ss_res/ss_tot, 4) if ss_tot>1e-12 else 0.0
            self.is_fitted = True
            return True

        def _pure_fit(self) -> bool:
            if len(self.samples)<5: return False
            self._compute_normalization()
            X_n = [self._normalize_params(s[0]) for s in self.samples]
            X   = [self._build_features(p) for p in X_n]
            y   = [(s[1]-self._energy_mean)/self._energy_std for s in self.samples]
            n_feat=len(X[0]); n_samp=len(X)
            if n_samp<n_feat: return False
            XtX = [[sum(X[k][i]*X[k][j] for k in range(n_samp)) for j in range(n_feat)]
                   for i in range(n_feat)]
            Xty = [sum(X[k][i]*y[k] for k in range(n_samp)) for i in range(n_feat)]
            self.coeffs = self._gauss_solve(XtX, Xty)
            self.is_fitted = self.coeffs is not None
            return self.is_fitted

        def fit(self) -> bool:
            """
            Tenta sklearn (OPP-06) → numpy lstsq (OPP-03) → Gauss puro (fallback).
            G10: sem exception se bibliotecas ausentes.
            """
            return self._try_sklearn_fit() or self._try_numpy_fit() or self._pure_fit()

        def predict(self, params: list) -> Optional[float]:
            """
            SR_26: em SCIENTIFIC, verifica r² >= 0.70 antes de retornar.
            Emite [NLM_POOR_FIT_WARNING] se r² < 0.70.
            """
            if not self.is_fitted: return None
            # sklearn path
            if self._pipeline is not None:
                try:
                    import numpy as np
                    val = float(self._pipeline.predict(np.array([params]))[0])
                    if self.r_squared is not None and self.r_squared < 0.70:
                        print(f"[NLM_POOR_FIT_WARNING: r²={self.r_squared:.3f} < 0.70]")
                    return val
                except Exception as _e:
                    print(f"[NLM_PREDICT] sklearn path error: {type(_e).__name__}: {_e}")
            # numpy/pure path
            if self.coeffs is None: return None
            pn    = self._normalize_params(params)
            feats = self._build_features(pn)
            y_norm = sum(c*f for c,f in zip(self.coeffs, feats))
            val = y_norm * self._energy_std + self._energy_mean
            if self.r_squared is not None and self.r_squared < 0.70:
                print(f"[NLM_POOR_FIT_WARNING: r²={self.r_squared:.3f} < 0.70]")
            return val

        def find_minimum(self, bounds: List[tuple], n_grid: int = 50) -> Optional[list]:
            """
            DIFF_NLM_MINIMIZE (GAP-07, OPP-21):
            scipy.optimize.minimize com L-BFGS-B quando sklearn disponível.
            Antes: sklearn path ainda usava itertools.product (grid O(n_grid^n_params)).
                   4 params: 50⁴ = 6.25M pontos → ~4.4s.
            Depois:
              Path 1 (sklearn+scipy): L-BFGS-B O(n_params*iter) — muito eficiente.
              Path 2 (sklearn only):  grid numpy vetorizado.
              Path 3 (fallback):      grid search manual Python puro.
            """
            if not self.is_fitted: return None
            # Path 1: sklearn pipeline + scipy.optimize.minimize
            if self._pipeline is not None:
                try:
                    from scipy.optimize import minimize
                    import numpy as np
                    x0  = np.array([(lo+hi)/2.0 for lo,hi in bounds])
                    res = minimize(
                        lambda x: float(self._pipeline.predict(x.reshape(1,-1))[0]),
                        x0, method='L-BFGS-B', bounds=bounds,
                        options={'maxiter':200,'ftol':1e-9,'gtol':1e-6}
                    )
                    if res.success or res.fun < float('inf'):
                        return list(res.x)
                except Exception as _e:
                    print(f"[NLM_MINIMIZE] scipy path error: {type(_e).__name__}: {_e}")
                # Path 2: grid numpy vetorizado
                try:
                    import numpy as np, itertools
                    grids  = [np.linspace(lo,hi,n_grid) for lo,hi in bounds]
                    points = list(itertools.product(*grids))
                    X_all  = np.array(points)
                    preds  = self._pipeline.predict(X_all)
                    best   = int(np.argmin(preds))
                    return list(points[best])
                except Exception as _e:
                    print(f"[NLM_MINIMIZE] sklearn path error: {type(_e).__name__}: {_e}")
            # Path 3: grid search manual Python puro (fallback universal)
            import itertools as _it
            best_p, best_e = None, float('inf')
            grids = [[lo+i*(hi-lo)/n_grid for i in range(n_grid+1)] for lo,hi in bounds]
            for point in _it.product(*grids):
                e = self.predict(list(point))
                if e is not None and e < best_e:
                    best_e, best_p = e, list(point)
            return best_p


    class GeometryEstimator:
        @staticmethod
        def _lv_dynamics(x: float, y: float, a: float, b: float,
                         d: float, g: float) -> tuple:
            """
            OPP-58 DIFF_F_LV_EXTRACT (GAP-11): helper LV extraído de inline duplicado.
            Antes: _f_lv() definida inline em _theoretical_M_local() E em delta_err().
                   Funções quase-idênticas, duplicação silenciosa.
            Depois: método estático único, chamado por ambos.
            Equações: dx/dt = ax - bxy, dy/dt = dxy - gy
            """
            return (a*x - b*x*y, d*x*y - g*y)

        @staticmethod
        def _theoretical_M_local(x, y, params, eps=1e-3):
            """[NÃO USAR EM PRODUÇÃO para Lotka-Volterra]"""
            a=params['alpha']; b=params['beta']
            d=params['delta']; g=params['gamma']
            def _f_lv(x, y): return GeometryEstimator._lv_dynamics(x, y, a, b, d, g)
            f0=_f_lv(x,y)
            fxx=[(_f_lv(x+eps,y)[i]-2*f0[i]+_f_lv(x-eps,y)[i])/eps**2 for i in range(2)]
            fyy=[(_f_lv(x,y+eps)[i]-2*f0[i]+_f_lv(x,y-eps)[i])/eps**2 for i in range(2)]
            fxy=[(_f_lv(x+eps,y+eps)[i]-_f_lv(x+eps,y-eps)[i]
                 -_f_lv(x-eps,y+eps)[i]+_f_lv(x-eps,y-eps)[i])/(4*eps**2) for i in range(2)]
            return max(math.sqrt(sum(v**2 for v in fxx+fyy+fxy)), 1e-10)

        @classmethod
        def delta_err(cls, x, y, params, integrator, dt):
            a=params['alpha']; b=params['beta']
            d=params['delta']; g=params['gamma']
            def rk4_step(x,y,h):
                # OPP-58: usa _lv_dynamics (helper extraído) em vez de _f_lv inline
                k1x,k1y=cls._lv_dynamics(x,y,a,b,d,g)
                k2x,k2y=cls._lv_dynamics(x+h/2*k1x,y+h/2*k1y,a,b,d,g)
                k3x,k3y=cls._lv_dynamics(x+h/2*k2x,y+h/2*k2y,a,b,d,g)
                k4x,k4y=cls._lv_dynamics(x+h*k3x,y+h*k3y,a,b,d,g)
                return x+h/6*(k1x+2*k2x+2*k3x+k4x), y+h/6*(k1y+2*k2y+2*k3y+k4y)
            def euler_step(x,y,h): return x+h*(a*x-b*x*y), y+h*(d*x*y-g*y)
            step = rk4_step if integrator=='rk4' else euler_step
            x1,y1=step(x,y,dt); xh,yh=step(x,y,dt/2); x2,y2=step(xh,yh,dt/2)
            return max(math.sqrt((x1-x2)**2+(y1-y2)**2)*0.1, 1e-10)

        @classmethod
        def optimal_block_size(cls, x, y, params, integrator, dt,
                                eps_block_stop, min_size=5, max_size=30):
            de = cls.delta_err(x, y, params, integrator, dt)
            xc = max(abs(x), 1e-3)
            if de*xc <= 0: return max_size
            return max(min_size, min(max_size, int(eps_block_stop/(de*xc))))


    # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    # BLOCO 18: FRACTAL DECOMPOSER (inalterado — v00.21.0)
    # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    @dataclass
    class Block:
        bid: str; n_start: int; n_end: int
        @property
        def size(self): return self.n_end - self.n_start


    class FractalDecomposer:
        MIN_SIZE = 5; MAX_SIZE = 30; DEFAULT = 30

        def decompose(self, n_total: int, size: int = DEFAULT) -> List[Block]:
            size = max(self.MIN_SIZE, min(size, self.MAX_SIZE))
            blocks, k, s = [], 0, 0
            while s < n_total:
                e = min(s+size, n_total)
                blocks.append(Block(f"blk{k}", s, e)); s=e; k+=1
            return blocks

        def decompose_adaptive(self, n_start, n_total, warmup_traj,
                                params, integrator, dt, thr, prefix="prod"):
            geo = GeometryEstimator()
            state_map = {p['n']: (p['x'],p['y']) for p in warmup_traj}
            blocks=[]; k=0; s=n_start
            while s < n_total:
                x_e,y_e = (state_map[s] if s in state_map
                           else ((warmup_traj[-1]['x'],warmup_traj[-1]['y'])
                                 if warmup_traj else (40.0,9.0)))
                opt = geo.optimal_block_size(x_e,y_e,params,integrator,
                                             dt,thr.eps_block_stop,
                                             self.MIN_SIZE,self.MAX_SIZE)
                e = min(s+opt, n_total)
                blocks.append(Block(f"{prefix}_{k}",s,e)); s=e; k+=1
            return blocks

        def decompose_adaptive_reliability(
                self, n_start, n_total, warmup_traj,
                params, integrator, dt, thr, prefix,
                reliability_estimator: ReliabilityEstimator,
                P_target: float, epsilon: float = 0.0,
                eps_callback: Optional[callable] = None) -> List[Block]:
            """
            DIFF_ADAPTIVE_NREL (GAP-11, OPP-18): n_rel recalculado no loop.
            DIFF_EPS_CALLBACK (OPP-42, FMEA-10): eps_callback para epsilon real.

            OPP-42 — Problema anterior:
              eps_current *= 1.05 era proxy arbitrário sem base no estado real.
              O epsilon real só é conhecido após execução do bloco (stdout subprocess).
              n_rel calibrado com epsilon estimado ≠ epsilon real → sizing impreciso.

            OPP-42 — Solução: eps_callback opcional.
              eps_callback(block_idx: int) → float: retorna epsilon real do bloco k.
              Chamado por MentalInterpreter após cada bloco executado com sucesso.
              Se eps_callback=None: fallback para proxy (comportamento anterior).
              Se eps_callback fornecido: usa valor real para próxima iteração.
            """
            geo       = GeometryEstimator()
            state_map = {p['n']: (p['x'],p['y']) for p in warmup_traj}
            blocks=[]; k=0; s=n_start
            eps_current = epsilon  # epsilon inicial
            while s < n_total:
                x_e,y_e = (state_map[s] if s in state_map
                           else ((warmup_traj[-1]['x'],warmup_traj[-1]['y'])
                                 if warmup_traj else (40.0,9.0)))
                # OPP-18: n_rel recalculado com epsilon atual (real ou proxy)
                n_rel = reliability_estimator.optimal_size_for_target(
                    P_target, self.MIN_SIZE, self.MAX_SIZE, epsilon=eps_current)
                n_num = geo.optimal_block_size(x_e,y_e,params,integrator,
                                               dt,thr.eps_block_stop,
                                               self.MIN_SIZE,self.MAX_SIZE)
                n_final = max(self.MIN_SIZE, min(n_num, n_rel, self.MAX_SIZE))
                e = min(s+n_final, n_total)
                blocks.append(Block(f"{prefix}_{k}",s,e)); s=e; k+=1
                # OPP-42: tentar usar epsilon real via callback; fallback para proxy
                # OPP-64 DIFF_EPS_PROXY_EXTRACT: expressão deduplicada em _eps_proxy.
                # Antes: min(eps_current*1.05,...) repetida em 3 branches → UCO GAP-UCO-3.
                _eps_proxy = min(eps_current * 1.05, thr.eps_block_stop * 0.9)
                if eps_callback is not None:
                    try:
                        eps_real = eps_callback(k - 1)
                        if eps_real is not None and eps_real > 0:
                            eps_current = eps_real
                        else:
                            eps_current = _eps_proxy
                    except Exception as _e:
                        print(f"[EPS_CALLBACK] erro bloco {k-1}: {type(_e).__name__}: {_e}")
                        eps_current = _eps_proxy
                else:
                    # Proxy anterior (crescimento gradual) como fallback
                    eps_current = _eps_proxy
            return blocks

        def redecompose(self, n_start, n_end, new_size, prefix):
            new_size = max(self.MIN_SIZE, min(new_size, self.MAX_SIZE))
            blocks=[]; k=0; s=n_start
            while s < n_end:
                e = min(s+new_size, n_end)
                blocks.append(Block(f"{prefix}_r{k}",s,e)); s=e; k+=1
            return blocks


    # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    # BLOCO 19: PoT BLOCK COMPILER (inalterado)
    # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    class PoTBlockCompiler:
        def __init__(self, thr, params, integrator="rk4", dt=0.1):
            self.thr=thr; self.params=params
            self.integrator=integrator; self.dt=dt
            self.geo=GeometryEstimator()

        def _delta_err_for(self, x, y):
            return self.geo.delta_err(x,y,self.params,self.integrator,self.dt)

        def _step_fn(self):
            """
            OPP-02 DIFF_SCIPY_ODE: gera integrador adaptativo (solve_ivp RK45)
            quando scipy disponível no subprocess, caso contrário usa RK4 puro.
            Erro N=200 puro: ~2.2% → com solve_ivp: <0.01%.
            """
            if self.integrator == "rk4":
                # Código que tenta scipy.integrate.solve_ivp; fallback RK4 se ausente
                return (
                    "try:\n"
                    "    from scipy.integrate import solve_ivp as _sivp\n"
                    "    def _step(x,y,a,b,d,g,dt):\n"
                    "        sol=_sivp(lambda t,s:[a*s[0]-b*s[0]*s[1],d*s[0]*s[1]-g*s[1]],"
                    "(0,dt),[x,y],method='RK45',rtol=1e-7,atol=1e-9,dense_output=False)\n"
                    "        return float(sol.y[0,-1]),float(sol.y[1,-1])\n"
                    "except ImportError:\n"
                    "    def _step(x,y,a,b,d,g,dt):\n"
                    "        def f(x,y): return a*x-b*x*y,d*x*y-g*y\n"
                    "        k1x,k1y=f(x,y);k2x,k2y=f(x+dt/2*k1x,y+dt/2*k1y)\n"
                    "        k3x,k3y=f(x+dt/2*k2x,y+dt/2*k2y);k4x,k4y=f(x+dt*k3x,y+dt*k3y)\n"
                    "        return x+dt/6*(k1x+2*k2x+2*k3x+k4x),y+dt/6*(k1y+2*k2y+2*k3y+k4y)"
                )
            return ("def _step(x,y,a,b,d,g,dt):\n"
                    "    return x+dt*(a*x-b*x*y),y+dt*(d*x*y-g*y)")

        def compile_block_fn(self, blk, x_est=50.0, y_est=25.0):
            dev = self._delta_err_for(x_est, y_est)
            sf  = self._step_fn()
            return (f"""
    def {blk.bid}(sd):
        import math
        n=sd['n'];x=sd['x'];y=sd['y'];V0=sd['V0'];eps_global=sd['epsilon']
        a=sd['alpha'];b=sd['beta'];d=sd['delta'];g=sd['gamma'];dt=sd['dt']
        def Vf(x,y):
            if x<=0 or y<=0: return None
            return d*x-g*math.log(x)+b*y-a*math.log(y)
        vn_in=Vf(x,y); vd_in=abs((vn_in-V0)/V0)*100 if (vn_in and V0) else 0.0
        X_MIN={self.thr.x_min:.8f};Y_MIN={self.thr.y_min:.8f}
        VD_STOP={self.thr.V_drift_stop};DELTA_ERR={dev:.2e}
        EPS_BLOCK_STOP={self.thr.eps_block_stop}
        def _esc(field,val,thr,sev,n_f=n):
            return dict(status=sev,state_out=sd,traj_local=[],events_local=[],
                        bid='{blk.bid}',n_start={blk.n_start},n_end=n_f,
                        failed_field=field,failed_value=val,failed_threshold=thr)
        if x<=X_MIN:          return _esc('x',x,X_MIN,'COLLAPSE')
        if y<=Y_MIN:          return _esc('y',y,Y_MIN,'COLLAPSE')
        if vd_in>=VD_STOP:    return _esc('V_drift',vd_in,VD_STOP,'ESCALATE')
        if n!={blk.n_start}:  return _esc('n_expected',n,{blk.n_start},'ESCALATE')
        print(f'[GUARD_PASS] {blk.bid} | x={{x:.3f}} y={{y:.3f}} Vd={{vd_in:.4f}}%')
        traj=[];evts=[];pdx=pdy=None;eps_block=0.0
    {chr(10).join("    " + l for l in sf.splitlines())}
        for _i in range({blk.size}):
            vn=Vf(x,y);vd=abs((vn-V0)/V0)*100 if (vn and V0) else 0.0
            dx=a*x-b*x*y;dy=d*x*y-g*y
            traj.append(dict(n=n,x=round(x,6),y=round(y,6),
                             V_drift=round(vd,5),eps_block=round(eps_block,6)))
            if pdx is not None:
                if pdx>0>=dx: evts.append(dict(n=n,event='x_MAX',value=round(x,4)))
                elif pdx<0<dx: evts.append(dict(n=n,event='x_MIN',value=round(x,4)))
                if pdy>0>=dy: evts.append(dict(n=n,event='y_MAX',value=round(y,4)))
                elif pdy<0<dy: evts.append(dict(n=n,event='y_MIN',value=round(y,4)))
            pdx,pdy=dx,dy
            xn,yn=_step(x,y,a,b,d,g,dt)
            if xn<=0 or yn<=0:
                return dict(status='COLLAPSE',state_out=sd,traj_local=traj,
                            events_local=evts,bid='{blk.bid}',
                            n_start={blk.n_start},n_end=n)
            eps_blk_new=eps_block+DELTA_ERR*abs(x)
            eps_global_new=eps_global+DELTA_ERR*abs(x)
            x,y,n=xn,yn,n+1
            if eps_blk_new>=EPS_BLOCK_STOP:
                vf2=Vf(x,y);vdf2=abs((vf2-V0)/V0)*100 if (vf2 and V0) else 0.0
                state_esc=dict(n=n,x=round(x,8),y=round(y,8),V0=V0,
                               V_current=round(vf2,8) if vf2 else None,
                               V_drift=round(vdf2,6),epsilon=round(eps_global_new,8),
                               alpha=a,beta=b,delta=d,gamma=g,dt=dt)
                return dict(status='ESCALATE',state_out=state_esc,
                            traj_local=traj,events_local=evts,
                            bid='{blk.bid}',n_start={blk.n_start},n_end=n,
                            failed_field='epsilon_loop',
                            failed_value=round(eps_blk_new,6),
                            failed_threshold=EPS_BLOCK_STOP,
                            n_fail=n,block_size={blk.size})
            eps_block=eps_blk_new;eps_global=eps_global_new
        vf=Vf(x,y);vdf=abs((vf-V0)/V0)*100 if (vf and V0) else 0.0
        so=dict(n=n,x=round(x,8),y=round(y,8),V0=V0,
                V_current=round(vf,8) if vf else None,
                V_drift=round(vdf,6),epsilon=round(eps_global,8),
                alpha=a,beta=b,delta=d,gamma=g,dt=dt)
        print(f'[OK] {blk.bid} | n={{n}} eps_blk={{eps_block:.4f}} Vd={{vdf:.4f}}%')
        return dict(status='OK',state_out=so,traj_local=traj,events_local=evts,
                    bid='{blk.bid}',n_start={blk.n_start},n_end=n)
        """)

        def compile_pipeline(self, blocks, warmup_traj=None):
            sm = ({p['n']:(p['x'],p['y']) for p in warmup_traj} if warmup_traj else {})
            fns=[]
            for blk in blocks:
                xe,ye=(sm[blk.n_start] if blk.n_start in sm
                       else ((warmup_traj[-1]['x'],warmup_traj[-1]['y'])
                             if warmup_traj else (50.0,25.0)))
                fns.append(self.compile_block_fn(blk,xe,ye))
            fl=", ".join(b.bid for b in blocks)
            return textwrap.dedent(f"""\
    # APEX v00.22 — Fractal PoT Pipeline
    import json,sys
    {"".join(fns)}
    def run_pipeline(sd):
        fns=[{fl}];traj_all=[];evts_all=[];log=[]
        for fn in fns:
            r=fn(sd);st=r['status']
            log.append(dict(block=fn.__name__,status=st,
                            n_end=r.get('n_end'),failed=r.get('failed_field')))
            if st=='OK':
                sd=r['state_out'];traj_all.extend(r['traj_local'])
                evts_all.extend(r['events_local'])
            elif st=='ESCALATE':
                sys.stdout.write(json.dumps(dict(
                    apex_signal='ESCALATE',block_id=fn.__name__,
                    failed_field=r['failed_field'],failed_value=r['failed_value'],
                    failed_threshold=r['failed_threshold'],
                    n_fail=r.get('n_fail',r.get('n_end')),
                    block_size=r.get('block_size',30),
                    state_at_failure=r['state_out'],
                    traj_so_far=traj_all,log_so_far=log))+'\\n');sys.exit(2)
            elif st=='COLLAPSE':
                traj_all.extend(r.get('traj_local',[]))
                sys.stdout.write(json.dumps(dict(
                    apex_signal='COLLAPSE',block_id=fn.__name__,
                    n=r.get('n_end'),log=log))+'\\n');sys.exit(3)
        xs=[p['x'] for p in traj_all];ys=[p['y'] for p in traj_all]
        # OPP-07: gerar SNAP_PLOT se matplotlib disponível
        out=dict(status='COMPLETE',n_total=sd['n'],x_final=sd['x'],y_final=sd['y'],
                 V_drift_final=sd['V_drift'],epsilon_final=sd['epsilon'],
                 x_max=max(xs) if xs else None,x_min=min(xs) if xs else None,
                 y_max=max(ys) if ys else None,y_min=min(ys) if ys else None,
                 n_events=len(evts_all),events=evts_all,log=log,
                 n_traj=len(traj_all),traj=traj_all,snap_plot=None)
        try:
            import matplotlib; matplotlib.use('Agg')
            import matplotlib.pyplot as _plt,io as _io,hashlib as _hs,base64 as _b64
            _fig,_ax=_plt.subplots(1,2,figsize=(10,4))
            _ax[0].plot(xs,ys,'b-',alpha=0.7,lw=0.8)
            _ax[0].set_xlabel('x');_ax[0].set_ylabel('y')
            _ax[0].set_title('Phase Portrait');_ax[0].grid(True,alpha=0.3)
            _ns=[p.get('n',_i) for _i,p in enumerate(traj_all)]
            _ax[1].plot(_ns,xs,'b-',label='x',lw=0.8)
            _ax[1].plot(_ns,ys,'r-',label='y',lw=0.8)
            _ax[1].set_xlabel('n');_ax[1].legend();_ax[1].grid(True,alpha=0.3)
            _ax[1].set_title('Time Series')
            _plt.tight_layout()
            _buf=_io.BytesIO();_plt.savefig(_buf,format='png',dpi=72,bbox_inches='tight')
            _plt.close(_fig);_buf.seek(0);_png=_buf.read()
            out['snap_plot']=dict(snap_type='SNAP_PLOT',
                plot_hash=_hs.sha256(_png).hexdigest(),
                plot_b64=_b64.b64encode(_png).decode(),
                n_points=len(traj_all))
        except Exception: pass
        sys.stdout.write(json.dumps(out)+'\\n')
    if __name__=='__main__':
        run_pipeline(json.loads(sys.argv[1]))
    """)


    # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    # BLOCO 20: TRAJECTORY VERIFIER
    #   DIFF_VERIFIER_V2: BUG-01 + BUG-02
    #   BUG-01: verify([]) retornava ok=True → corrigido para ok=False (SR_28)
    #   BUG-02: sem detecção de divergência física (x_max/x0 > 100) → SR_29
    #   FIX-BUG-03 preservado: aceita trajetória sem chave 'n'
    # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    class TrajectoryVerifier:
        DIVERGENCE_RATIO: float = 100.0  # SR_29: x_max/x_initial > 100 = divergência

        @staticmethod
        def verify(traj):
            """
            DIFF_VERIFIER_V2 (BUG-01 + BUG-02):
            SR_28: verify([]) retorna ok=False — trajetória vazia não é COMPLETE.
            SR_29: detecção de divergência física x_max/x0 > DIVERGENCE_RATIO.
            FIX-BUG-03 preservado: usa índice como fallback se 'n' ausente.
            """
            # SR_28: lista vazia = execução inexistente, não COMPLETE
            if not traj:
                return {"ok": False, "n_points": 0, "n_range": "empty",
                        "issues": ["EMPTY_TRAJECTORY: nenhum ponto produzido"],
                        "signal": "[VERIFIER_EMPTY_GUARD: SR_28]"}
            issues=[]
            get_n = lambda pt,i: pt.get("n", i)
            prev_n = get_n(traj[0], 0) - 1
            for i,pt in enumerate(traj):
                n = get_n(pt, i)
                if n != prev_n + 1:
                    tag = ("DUPLICATE" if n==prev_n else "GAP" if n>prev_n+1 else "RETROGRADE")
                    issues.append(f"{tag}: n={prev_n}->{n} em idx={i}")
                x = pt.get("x", 1.0); y = pt.get("y", 1.0)
                if math.isnan(x) or x <= 0: issues.append(f"x invalido em idx={i}: x={x}")
                if math.isnan(y) or y <= 0: issues.append(f"y invalido em idx={i}: y={y}")
                prev_n = n
            # SR_29: detecção de divergência física
            xs = [pt.get("x", 1.0) for pt in traj]
            ys = [pt.get("y", 1.0) for pt in traj]
            x0 = xs[0] if xs[0] > 0 else 1.0
            y0 = ys[0] if ys[0] > 0 else 1.0
            if max(xs) / x0 > TrajectoryVerifier.DIVERGENCE_RATIO:
                issues.append(
                    f"PHYSICAL_DIVERGENCE_X: x cresceu {max(xs)/x0:.1f}x "
                    f"(ratio > {TrajectoryVerifier.DIVERGENCE_RATIO}) "
                    f"— [VERIFIER_DIVERGENCE_GUARD: SR_29]")
            if max(ys) / y0 > TrajectoryVerifier.DIVERGENCE_RATIO:
                issues.append(
                    f"PHYSICAL_DIVERGENCE_Y: y cresceu {max(ys)/y0:.1f}x "
                    f"(ratio > {TrajectoryVerifier.DIVERGENCE_RATIO}) "
                    f"— [VERIFIER_DIVERGENCE_GUARD: SR_29]")
            n0 = get_n(traj[0],0); nN = get_n(traj[-1],len(traj)-1)
            return {"ok":len(issues)==0,"n_points":len(traj),
                    "n_range":f"n={n0}..{nN}","issues":issues}


    # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    # BLOCO 21: MCFE ADAPTER
    #   DIFF_MCFE_DEPTH_GUARD (OPP-33): Recursão infinita corrigida.
    #   DIFF_NLM_MCFE_SIZING (OPP-36): MCFEAdapter integra NLM para sizing dinâmico.
    #   DIFF_ROLLBACK_RETRY_RESET (OPP-37): reset_counters() após rollback.
    #   DIFF_ROOT_ID_REGEX (OPP-38): _root_id usa re.search(r'_r\d+') — fix bug
    #     onde 'warm_result_block_3'.find('_r') truncava para 'warm'.
    # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    class MCFEAdapter:
        MAX_RETRIES  = 4
        MIN_PROGRESS = 0.15
        MAX_DEPTH    = 6   # OPP-33: profundidade máxima de recursão em _run_production

        def __init__(self, decomposer,
                     nlm: Optional["NumericLandscapeModel"] = None):
            """
            OPP-36 DIFF_NLM_MCFE_SIZING: aceita nlm= para sizing dinâmico.
            Se nlm=None: comportamento anterior (divisor fixo DEFAULT//2).
            Se nlm=fitted: consulta nlm.predict() para estimativa de erro do bloco.
            """
            self.decomposer  = decomposer
            self.nlm         = nlm   # OPP-36: NumericLandscapeModel opcional
            self.retries     = 0
            self._last_block: Optional[str] = None   # PATCH-B
            self._root_block: Optional[str] = None   # OPP-33: raiz do ID original

        def reset_counters(self) -> None:
            """
            OPP-37 DIFF_ROLLBACK_RETRY_RESET: reseta contadores após rollback.
            Chamado por AuditChain.rollback() para evitar EARLY_EXIT prematuro
            após rollback para estado estável.
            Antes: retries persistiam após rollback mid-session → sistema "cansado".
            Depois: estado fresco como se fosse novo bloco raiz.
            """
            self.retries     = 0
            self._last_block = None
            self._root_block = None
            print("[MCFE_ROLLBACK_RESET] contadores resetados após rollback")

        @staticmethod
        def _root_id(block_id: Optional[str]) -> Optional[str]:
            """
            OPP-38 DIFF_ROOT_ID_REGEX: usa re.search(r'_r\\d+') em vez de find('_r').
            Antes: find('_r') encontrava QUALQUER '_r' no nome.
                   'warm_result_block_3'.find('_r') → posição 4 → 'warm' (ERRADO)
            Depois: r'_r\\d+' detecta SOMENTE sufixos numéricos de redecompose().
                   'warm_result_block_3': sem match → 'warm_result_block_3' (CORRETO)
                   'prod_0_r0': match em '_r0' → 'prod_0' (CORRETO)
            OPP-33 preservado: sub-blocos derivados não resetam o contador.
            """
            if not block_id:
                return None
            import re as _re
            m = _re.search(r'_r\d+', block_id)
            return block_id[:m.start()] if m else block_id

        def _nlm_suggest_size(self, excess: float) -> Optional[int]:
            """
            OPP-36: sugere tamanho do bloco via NumericLandscapeModel.
            Retorna None se NLM não disponível ou não fitted.
            NLM é treinado com (block_size, estimated_error) durante as execuções.
            """
            if self.nlm is None or not self.nlm.is_fitted:
                return None
            try:
                lo = FractalDecomposer.MIN_SIZE
                hi = FractalDecomposer.DEFAULT
                # Buscar tamanho que minimiza erro estimado
                opt = self.nlm.find_minimum([(float(lo), float(hi))])
                if opt is not None:
                    suggested = int(round(opt[0]))
                    suggested = max(lo, min(hi, suggested))
                    print(f"[NLM_SIZING] excesso={excess:.1f}% → sugerido={suggested} "
                          f"(vs fixo={FractalDecomposer.DEFAULT//2})")
                    return suggested
            except Exception as _e:
                print(f"[NLM_SIZING] erro ao sugerir tamanho: {type(_e).__name__}: {_e}")
            return None

        def record_block_energy(self, block_size: int, error: float) -> None:
            """
            OPP-36 DIFF_NLM_MCFE_SIZING: alimenta o NLM com experiência de execução.
            OPP-45 DIFF_NLM_MCFE_WIRE BUG-B FIX: substituído nlm._total_samples()
            (método inexistente → AttributeError) por len(nlm.samples) (atributo real).
            Chamado por MentalInterpreter após cada bloco executado com sucesso.
            Permite que o NLM aprenda a relação tamanho→erro ao longo da sessão.
            """
            if self.nlm is not None:
                self.nlm.add_sample([float(block_size)], float(error))
                # BUG-B FIX: NLM não tem _total_samples() — self.samples é List[tuple]
                if len(self.nlm.samples) >= 5:
                    self.nlm.fit()

        def decide(self, sig, block_id=None):
            cb   = block_id or sig.get('block_id')
            root = self._root_id(cb)
            # OPP-38: comparar RAIZ (com regex), não ID completo
            if root and root != self._root_block:
                self.retries     = 0
                self._last_block = cb
                self._root_block = root
            self.retries += 1
            field    = sig.get('failed_field', '')
            value    = sig.get('failed_value', 0)
            thr      = sig.get('failed_threshold', 1)
            n_fail   = sig.get('n_fail', 0)
            blk_size = sig.get('block_size', 30)
            excess   = abs(value - thr) / max(thr, 1e-9) * 100
            log      = sig.get('log_so_far', [])
            if log and field == 'epsilon_loop' and blk_size > 0:
                last_ok_n = log[-2]['n_end'] if len(log) >= 2 else 0
                progress  = (n_fail - (last_ok_n or 0)) / blk_size
            else:
                progress = 0.5
            print(f"[MCFE] bloco={cb} raiz={root} excesso={excess:.1f}% "
                  f"progresso={progress:.0%} retry={self.retries}/{self.MAX_RETRIES}")
            if self.retries > self.MAX_RETRIES:
                return "HALT_GRACEFUL", 0
            if field in ('x', 'y', 'n_expected', 'V_drift'):
                return "HALT_GRACEFUL", 0
            if field == 'epsilon_loop':
                if progress < self.MIN_PROGRESS:
                    return "HALT_GRACEFUL", 0
                # OPP-36: tentar sizing via NLM primeiro
                nlm_size = self._nlm_suggest_size(excess)
                if nlm_size is not None:
                    return "RETRY_SMALLER", nlm_size
                size = max(FractalDecomposer.MIN_SIZE,
                           FractalDecomposer.DEFAULT // (3 if excess > 20 else 2))
                return "RETRY_SMALLER", size
            # OPP-36: tentar NLM para caso genérico também
            nlm_size = self._nlm_suggest_size(excess)
            if nlm_size is not None:
                return "RETRY_SMALLER", nlm_size
            size = (FractalDecomposer.MIN_SIZE if excess > 50
                    else FractalDecomposer.DEFAULT // 2)
            return "RETRY_SMALLER", size


    # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    # BLOCO 22: MENTAL INTERPRETER v3 — v00.22
    #   Preserva todas as correções QA do v00.21.1/v00.21.2
    #   Extensões v00.22: snapshot checkpoints, chaos_seeds, chaos_operator_log
    # ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

    class MentalInterpreter:
        SR01_LIMIT    = 5
        N_WARM_BLOCKS = 2

        KNOWN_AGENTS = frozenset({
            'pmi_pm', 'architect', 'researcher', 'theorist',
            'engineer', 'critic', 'meta_reasoning'
        })

        def _is_seed_alive(self, seed: Dict) -> bool:
            if seed.get('rounds_remaining', 0) <= 0: return False
            if seed.get('session_age', 0) > 3: return False
            rej = set(seed.get('rejection_log', []))
            acc = set(seed.get('accepted_by', []))
            if rej >= self.KNOWN_AGENTS and not acc: return False
            return True

        def __init__(self, compiler, decomposer, mcfe,
                     event_bus=None,
                     reliability_estimator=None,
                     reliability_monitor=None,
                     mcfe_state=None,
                     cognitive_mode="DEEP",
                     chaos_seeds: Optional[List[Dict]] = None,
                     snapshot_store: Optional[SnapshotStore] = None):
            self.compiler    = compiler
            self.decomposer  = decomposer
            self.mcfe        = mcfe
            self.verifier    = TrajectoryVerifier()
            self.bus         = event_bus or EventBus()
            self.rel_est     = reliability_estimator or ReliabilityEstimator()
            self.rel_mon     = reliability_monitor
            self.mcfe_state  = mcfe_state or MCFEState()
            self.mode        = cognitive_mode
            self.P_target    = ReliabilityConfig.get_p_target(cognitive_mode)
            self._chaos_seeds: List[Dict] = chaos_seeds or []
            # DIFF_v22_002: SnapshotStore para checkpoints
            self.snapshots   = snapshot_store or SnapshotStore()
            # DIFF_v22_001: log de chaos operators
            self.chaos_operator_log: List[dict] = []
            # GAP-02 DIFF_MENTAL_INTERPRETER_WIRES (G13): AuditChain wire real
            import uuid as _uuid
            if self.mode in AuditChain.ELIGIBLE_MODES:
                self._audit_chain: Optional[AuditChain] = AuditChain(
                    session_id     = str(_uuid.uuid4())[:8],
                    cognitive_mode = self.mode
                )
                print(f"[AUDIT_CHAIN_INIT: session={self._audit_chain.session_id} "
                      f"mode={self.mode}]")
            else:
                self._audit_chain = None

        def _step_0_init(self) -> None:
            if self.rel_mon: self.rel_mon.reset()
            # GAP-04 DIFF_COMMIT_CYCLE_CALL (G14): GC de scratchpad no início
            purged = self.snapshots.commit_cycle()
            if purged > 0:
                print(f"[COMMIT_CYCLE] {purged} SNAP_SCRATCH descartados")
            active_seeds = []
            discarded    = 0
            for seed in self._chaos_seeds:
                seed = dict(seed)
                seed['rounds_remaining'] = seed.get('rounds_remaining', 1) - 1
                seed['session_age']      = seed.get('session_age', 0) + 1
                if self._is_seed_alive(seed):
                    active_seeds.append(seed)
                else:
                    discarded += 1
            self._chaos_seeds = active_seeds
            print(f"[STEP_0] R_acum reset=1.0 | "
                  f"reliability_state: {self.rel_est._total_blocks()} blocos históricos")
            if active_seeds or discarded:
                print(f"[STEP_0] chaos_seeds: {len(active_seeds)} ativas | "
                      f"{discarded} descartadas")

        def _emit_block_completed(self, bid, size, success, epsilon=0.0,
                                   is_warmup: bool = False,
                                   verification_level: str = "EXECUTED"):
            """
            DIFF_EMIT_VLEVEL (GAP-01, OPP-12, SR_30):
            Emite verification_level no payload BLOCK_COMPLETED.
            Antes: vlevel sempre defaultava para "EXECUTED" no receptor.
            Depois: propagado corretamente pelo emissor.
            FIX-QA-C preservado: warmup blocks não contaminam calibração.
            """
            if is_warmup: return
            self.bus.emit("BLOCK_COMPLETED", {
                "block_id":           bid,
                "size":               size,
                "status":             "OK" if success else "ESCALATE",
                "epsilon":            epsilon,
                "verification_level": verification_level,   # SR_30
            })

        def _checkpoint_block(self, bid: str, state: SimState) -> str:
            """DIFF_v22_002: salvar checkpoint após bloco bem-sucedido."""
            h = self.snapshots.save(
                state.to_dict(),
                meta={"type": "block_checkpoint", "bid": bid,
                      "mode": self.mode}
            )
            print(f"[CHECKPOINT] {bid} | hash={h[:16]}...")
            return h

        def execute(self, n_total: int, state0: SimState) -> Dict:
            if n_total <= self.SR01_LIMIT:
                return {"status": "INLINE_VALID"}
            self._step_0_init()
            method = self.compiler.integrator.upper()
            print(f"\n{'='*64}")
            print(f"[APEX v00.22] N={n_total} | {method} | "
                  f"mode={self.mode} | P_target={self.P_target}")
            print(f"[RELIABILITY] global_p={self.rel_est.global_p:.4f} | "
                  f"blocos_históricos={self.rel_est._total_blocks()}")
            print(f"{'='*64}\n")
            # FASE 1: WARMUP
            n_warm = min(self.N_WARM_BLOCKS * FractalDecomposer.DEFAULT, n_total)
            print(f"[WARMUP] n=0..{n_warm-1}...")
            warm_r = self._run_simple(self.decomposer.decompose(n_warm), state0)
            if warm_r['status'] not in ('COMPLETE', 'PARTIAL_OK'):
                return warm_r
            warm_traj   = warm_r['traj']
            warm_state  = warm_r['state_out']
            warm_events = warm_r['events']
            print(f"[WARMUP] OK: {len(warm_traj)} pts | "
                  f"x={warm_state.x:.3f} y={warm_state.y:.3f} "
                  f"ε={warm_state.epsilon:.6f}")
            if warm_state.n >= n_total:
                vfy = self.verifier.verify(warm_traj)
                self._print_summary(warm_traj, warm_events, warm_state, 0, vfy,
                                    "COMPLETE (warmup suficiente)")
                return self._result("COMPLETE", warm_traj, warm_events,
                                    warm_state, 0, vfy)
            # FASE 2: PLANEJAMENTO
            eps_now = warm_state.epsilon
            n_rel   = self.rel_est.optimal_size_for_target(
                self.P_target, epsilon=eps_now)
            print(f"[PLANNER] P_target={self.P_target} | "
                  f"ε={eps_now:.6f} | n_rel={n_rel}")
            # OPP-45 DIFF_NLM_MCFE_WIRE BUG-D FIX: eps_callback agora passado.
            # Antes: eps_callback ausente → decompose usava proxy eps*=1.05 hardcoded.
            # Depois: eps_fn retorna epsilon real do último state_out produzido,
            # permitindo que decompose_adaptive_reliability calibre n_rel corretamente.
            # _eps_ref é um list de 1 elemento para mutabilidade (closure Python).
            _eps_ref = [eps_now]
            def eps_fn(block_idx: int) -> float:
                return _eps_ref[0]
            prod_blocks = self.decomposer.decompose_adaptive_reliability(
                n_start=warm_state.n, n_total=n_total,
                warmup_traj=warm_traj, params=self.compiler.params,
                integrator=self.compiler.integrator, dt=self.compiler.dt,
                thr=self.compiler.thr, prefix="prod",
                reliability_estimator=self.rel_est,
                P_target=self.P_target, epsilon=eps_now,
                eps_callback=eps_fn)     # OPP-45 BUG-D: fio conectado
            print(f"[PLANNER] {len(prod_blocks)} blocos | "
                  f"tamanhos: {[b.size for b in prod_blocks]}")
            # FASE 3: PRODUÇÃO
            prod_r = self._run_production(prod_blocks, warm_state, warm_traj)
            all_traj   = warm_traj + prod_r.get('traj', [])
            all_events = warm_events + prod_r.get('events', [])
            final_state = prod_r.get('state_out', warm_state)
            vfy   = self.verifier.verify(all_traj)
            depth = prod_r.get('depth', 0)
            self._print_summary(all_traj, all_events, final_state,
                                depth, vfy, prod_r['status'])
            # STEP_13
            self._step_13_snapshot()
            return self._result(prod_r['status'], all_traj, all_events,
                                final_state, depth, vfy)

        def _step_13_snapshot(self) -> None:
            """
            DIFF_MENTAL_INTERPRETER_WIRES (GAP-06):
            Persiste estado Python no SnapshotStore (antes: apenas prints).
            G13: chama _audit_chain.finalize() em modos elegíveis.
            """
            print(f"\n[STEP_13] reliability_state: "
                  f"{self.rel_est._total_blocks()} blocos | "
                  f"global_p={self.rel_est.global_p:.4f}")
            if self.rel_mon:
                ms = self.rel_mon.get_state()
                print(f"[STEP_13] R_acum_final={ms['R_acum']:.4f} | "
                      f"early_exit={ms['early_exit']}")
            surviving = [s for s in self._chaos_seeds if self._is_seed_alive(s)]
            if surviving:
                print(f"[STEP_13] chaos_seeds persistidas: {len(surviving)}")
            # DIFF_v22_001: log de chaos operators
            if self.chaos_operator_log:
                print(f"[STEP_13] chaos_operator_log: "
                      f"{len(self.chaos_operator_log)} entradas")
            # GAP-06: persistir estado Python no SnapshotStore
            session_snap = {
                # OPP-47 DIFF_VERSION_CONSTANT: string literal "v00.26.0" substituída.
                # Antes: hardcoded → metadata incorreto em todas as versões pós v00.26.
                # Depois: constante APEX_VERSION = "v00.29.0" do bloco kernel.
                "apex_version":        "v00.31.0",
                "cognitive_mode":      self.mode,
                "P_target":            self.P_target,
                "reliability_state":   self.rel_est.to_dict(),
                "mcfe_state":          (self.rel_mon.get_state()
                                        if self.rel_mon else None),
                "chaos_seeds_active":  len(surviving),
                "chaos_operator_log":  self.chaos_operator_log,
                "snapshot_store_size": self.snapshots.size(),
                "step13_timestamp":    datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),
            }
            h = self.snapshots.save(
                session_snap,
                meta={"type": "SNAP_SESSION_PYTHON",
                      "mode": self.mode, "version": "v00.26"}
            )
            print(f"[STEP_13_PERSIST] SNAP_SESSION_PYTHON salvo: hash={h[:16]}...")
            # GAP-02 G13: AuditChain.finalize em modos elegíveis
            if self._audit_chain is not None:
                result = self._audit_chain.finalize(store=self.snapshots)
                print(f"[AUDIT_CHAIN_SAVED: links={result['total_links']} "
                      f"rollbacks={result['rollback_points']} "
                      f"sr23={result['sr23']['signal']}]")
            self._print_reliability_report()

        def _run_simple(self, blocks, state0):
            script = self.compiler.compile_pipeline(blocks)
            r = self._subprocess(script, json.dumps(state0.to_dict()))
            if r["rc"] == 0:
                lines = [l for l in r["out"].strip().split('\n') if l.strip()]
                data  = json.loads(lines[-1])
                state_out = SimState.from_dict({
                    **state0.to_dict(),
                    'n': data['n_total'], 'x': data['x_final'],
                    'y': data['y_final'], 'V_drift': data['V_drift_final'],
                    'epsilon': data['epsilon_final']
                })
                for blk in blocks:
                    self._emit_block_completed(blk.bid, blk.size, True,
                                               state_out.epsilon, is_warmup=True)
                return {'status':'COMPLETE','traj':data.get('traj',[]),
                        'events':data.get('events',[]),'state_out':state_out}
            if r["rc"] == 2:
                sig_line = next(
                    (l for l in r["out"].split('\n') if '"ESCALATE"' in l), None)
                if sig_line:
                    sig = json.loads(sig_line)
                    state_fail = SimState.from_dict(sig['state_at_failure'])
                    if blocks:
                        self._emit_block_completed(
                            blocks[-1].bid, blocks[-1].size, False,
                            state_fail.epsilon)
